Basic Work of College and Career Guidance (Part 1) 149

— He Jirou

Educators today are all paying attention to the issue of students' future paths, because students' future paths are an important indicator of the effectiveness of education. Especially middle school educators are more concerned about the issue of graduation and further studies or employment, because middle school students feel these two issues most deeply, and appropriate solutions are even more related to the overall effectiveness of education. Therefore, those who advocate guidance pay more attention to the guidance of middle school students in further studies and employment.

There are only two paths for middle school students: further studies and employment. Ideally, graduates of vocational schools and normal schools should naturally all be employed. However, in reality, there are always a few who, due to various circumstances, change their career plans and seek higher knowledge, so there is also the issue of further studies. As for ordinary middle schools, they are originally intended to prepare students for further studies, but among the graduates, there are inevitably various difficulties that prevent them from continuing their education and require them to enter society to make a living. Therefore, the employment issue still exists. The nature of these two issues is continuous, and some of the principles for solving them are common, so they can be discussed together.

Since the Ministry of Education announced the "Measures for Guidance on Further Studies and Employment in Primary and Secondary Schools" in the 22nd year, attention to guidance work in various places has increased a lot. Many schools are working hard to implement it and are proceeding in accordance with the key points set by the ministry. However, it is feared that not many can fully implement all the matters listed in the measures, or perhaps none. (The China Vocational Education Society is currently investigating the implementation of guidance in secondary schools.) There are naturally some schools that have achieved considerable results in implementing guidance, but there are also quite a few that have not achieved any results. The reasons for the limited achievements are roughly due to several incorrect ideas:

1. Perfunctory Response: Some who implement guidance work do not recognize the importance of this work and do not have the determination to implement it. Since the educational administrative organs have orders, they have no choice but to respond perfunctorily to fulfill their responsibilities. They either organize committees, or hold lectures, or have other activities, but all of these are just materials to be reported. They do not grasp the essentials of student guidance and do not implement it effectively, so the results are superficial and almost zero.

2. Superficial Publicity: Some education officials have no research on guidance work and fail to understand its meaning and important methods. However, upon hearing someone advocate guidance work, they think it is novel, or seeing other schools organize guidance programs, they are motivated by a competitive mentality. So they also add some guidance activities as embellishments and publicity materials. As for the real benefits that students gain, they cannot be taken into consideration.

3. Temporary First Aid: Some educators believe that guidance work is a temporary relief effort specifically for the period close to graduation. When the issue of students' future paths becomes urgent near graduation, attention is drawn to guidance. Lectures are held, contacts are made, senior school situations are investigated, and they have to be busy for a while. However, after the graduation period, they put this matter aside again, thinking it is not important.

The above-mentioned concepts naturally arise because the meaning and nature of guidance work are not fundamentally recognized. The important and valuable aspects of guidance implementation cannot be distinguished. If this continues, guidance work will not be effective and will not make progress. All advocacy will become empty talk, and all implementation will become blind. To correct the several incorrect concepts mentioned above, there are several principles regarding guidance that should be specially mentioned here:

1. Guidance is Part of Education: Guidance on further studies or employment is often thought of as work outside of formal education. In reality, guidance is education. Schools implement education in order to cultivate talents. If students cannot receive proper further education, and those seeking employment cannot find suitable careers, the effectiveness of education can be considered completely lost. All educational activities are meaningless. Therefore, guidance work must be carried out in conjunction with other educational activities and become an equally important part.

2. Guidance is Everyday Work: Guidance on further studies and employment is needed when facing the issue of future paths, and the issue of future paths superficially belongs to a certain time. Therefore, some people think that guidance work is also seasonal and that holding it once every summer vacation is enough. Although the actual solution of future paths is near graduation, the success of guidance depends entirely on the facilities established on weekdays. It cannot be obtained by sharpening the spear just before the battle, because to solve the problem of further studies or employment, it is necessary to understand the individual's past and present situation, as well as the situation of schools and occupations. And the method of handling it requires a lot of long-term preparation, which cannot be completed temporarily. Therefore, guidance work is long-term, continuous, and proceeds simultaneously with everyday education.

3. Guidance Emphasizes Individual Treatment: The methods of guidance work can be divided into group and individual in terms of organization. Common guidance for the majority of people, such as publications and lectures, can be said to be group guidance. Individual treatment according to the individual's situation and problems can be called individual guidance. Although group guidance cannot be considered ineffective, it will produce very little results if it is not supplemented by individual guidance. Individual guidance is the center of the work and cannot be eliminated, so it should be given special emphasis.

By affirming these principles, the several incorrect concepts mentioned earlier can naturally be corrected. Other principles do not need to be discussed here. But after recognizing the meaning and importance of guidance, how should it be implemented? What are some things that should be implemented in order to solve the problem of students' further studies and employment? The answer to this question is very broad, and many have already been listed in the outline of the methods set by the Ministry of Education, which are very thorough. This article does not intend to offer a complete answer, but only briefly explains several basic tasks for secondary schools to assist students in solving the problem of further studies and employment. (To be continued)

Sports News

Before the Opening of the World Games: A Grand Celebration Performance Will Be Held: Featuring Six Kinds of Singing and Dancing Programs; 10,000 Adults and Tens of Thousands of Children Will Participate 151

(Berlin News) The World Olympic Games, which will be held in Berlin in August of this year, has been prepared by Dr. Nitzsche-Gerhard to hold a large-scale celebration meeting, which is scheduled to be performed on the opening day. In the past, Dr. Gerhard has been responsible for the preparation of the Hant Memorial Meeting in Göttingen, the National Day Memorial Meeting in Heidelberg, etc. Later, he served as a director at the New York City Opera for three years. After returning to China, he served as the preparation of the Cologne National Day Memorial Meeting and founded the National Grand Theater in 1934.

This celebration performance was suggested by Sir Corbden. 12,000 adults and tens of thousands of children will participate in the performance. There are six types of programs, ranging from children's games to solemn singing. This kind of performance cannot be limited to gymnastics, but it cannot be too literary. The most difficult part is the problem of the scenery. It is difficult to avoid various difficulties when performing artistic singing and dancing in a sports field. For example, props, lighting, etc. must be designed by experts in order to be suitable for a large audience. In addition, designed by architectural experts, the venue will be divided into several parts, so that the oval venue becomes a circular or square stage to suit the artistic performance. At the same time, the use of light, color and scenery will make the venue undergo various changes.

The first act of the performance is "Olympic Flag Dance," which uses children's dance movements to perform the shape of the Olympic flag.

The second act is "Solemnity and Purity," in which 2,100 girls participate in the performance. First, a girl decorated as "Baruca" performs a waltz, followed by 500 female students from Berlin universities performing various games with wooden balls, iron rings, and pointed sticks.

The third act is "Work and Games," in which 2,000 students and representatives from various countries participate in the performance. The scenery is the camping life of various countries. Representatives from various countries sing their national folk songs, which are broadcast throughout the venue through loudspeakers and illuminated by searchlights. Finally, children from various countries parade around the venue for a week, and three Swiss children's consuls lead a flag exercise of 1,200 people.

The fourth act is "Strength and Agility," performed by 1,000 soldiers and 500 athletes, including mechanical exercises, javelin, and iron ball items.

The fifth act is "Victory," performed by sixty of Germany's best male dancers. The dancers are dressed as two teams of warriors. The two leaders hold a sword fight. Finally, the warrior decorated by Gotzburg is defeated by the sword. Then, eighty dancers led by Mary Wigman come out and dance, placing the dead at the feet of the victor. Finally, the Berlin Grand Orchestra plays "The Olympic Song." All the singing groups in Berlin lead the dancers and children holding torches into the venue. At the same time, the flags and emblems of various countries are arranged in a circle around the venue, and the space is interwoven with strong searchlights to form patterns. In the sound of Beethoven's Ninth Symphony, combined with the song "Joy—the Bright Light of God's Daughter," the horns are full, and the cheers are resounding. In the meantime, the solemn bell of "The Olympic Bell" seems to tell people that "I will awaken the youth of the world."

In the cotton yarn market this morning, the market was initially restrained due to the global cotton yarn situation trending downward. At the same time, spot yarn demand was weak, causing general retail investors to sell off and the market to decline. In the afternoon, due to a sharp rise in old cotton, multiple parties came in to drive up prices. By the time of the third closing, the market had turned to soar.

The marked yarn market opened this morning with prices falling across the board due to the overseas cotton yarn market situation. The decline intensified, and retail investors in the market unanimously bearishly sold off, with each falling by 8 jiao to 1 yuan, 2 jiao, 3 fen. After a consolidation in the second session, it was heard that old cotton was firm, and prices suddenly rebounded by 1 yuan to 8 jiao, 9 fen. The third closing showed weakness due to the lack of spot yarn business and a sharp drop of 23 yuan in Osaka Sampin yarn. Yesterday, the cotton fabric market saw improved sentiment among Cantonese merchants due to hopes for peace in the southwest situation and the sharp rise in the Cantonese currency. Cantonese merchants, known for their strong sales in the region of native fine twills, inquired about prices, leading to a slightly more active market. Although sales prices have not officially increased, asking prices have risen by about five cents. Yesterday, over 300 bales of fine twills from this factory and over 200 bales of fine and coarse cloth from this factory were brought in. The market saw brisk sales only for fine twills from this factory and lower-grade fine cloth from this factory, while other domestic textiles remained weak. Twelve-pound fine cloth reportedly fell slightly by 2.5 cents per piece, and ten-pound market cloth also showed slight weakness, varying from 2.5 to 5 cents. Yesterday, Fujian merchants added over 200 pieces of assorted plain and patterned broadcloth, straight tribute cloth, fine cloth, fine twills, blue cloth, and yuan twills. The Luzhou guild purchased over 100 pieces of Hongmai factory's Three Rams straight tribute cloth, broadcloth, fine cloth, and fine twills. Other merchants added only small quantities.

Woolen Goods Sales Slow, Prices Remain Firm 175

Yesterday, demand for woolen goods from local merchants was met, and sales prices remained firm. Summer gauze wool and linen textiles remained stable, likely due to limited inventory and strong market confidence. Yesterday, common Saigon hemp canvas was offered at a uniform price of $2.25, wide white single yarn canvas at 54 cents, red-patterned white broadcloth at $3.50, Yiji brand broadcloth at $4.75, valentino at $4.40. Pure white, a popular item, was scarce and commanded a premium. Yellow twill Dafeng domestic product sold for 49 cents, Renchang Japanese product for 46.5 cents, Tianxiang British product for 62 cents, and Haohua tea green for 74 cents.

Silk and Tea: Yokohama Futures and Spot Silk Rise – Slight Retraction in US and France 176

Yesterday, overseas silk prices retracted slightly. Prices for Chinese and Japanese silk in New York fell by two cents per pound each. Spot prices rose slightly by one cent, while futures fell by about half a cent from the previous day. Lyon Japanese silk fell by half a franc, while other prices remained unchanged. Sentiment in Yokohama was better, with spot prices rising by 2.5 yuan and futures by 11 yuan. Yesterday, Shanghai foreign silk firms saw only Dachang take in ten bales of gray silk, while white silk transactions only saw slightly improved appetite from customers.

Qimen Floral Fragrance Tea Exports to England Revive - Various Grades of Chun Mei Sell Well This Week 177

Yesterday, exports of Qimen floral fragrance black tea to England revived. The Jardine Matheson trading company purchased over 600 boxes at a price of 34-35 yuan, a decrease of 6-7 yuan from the previous price. However, the black tea market still lacks significant improvement. Chun Mei green tea sales remain active, with Xiehe, Tongfu, Jinlong, Baochang, and other firms purchasing large quantities. Needle Mei and pearl tea also sold well, while Gongxi green tea remained stagnant.

Furthermore, according to the Tea Merchants' Association report, various grades of Chun Mei sold well this week. Due to the superior quality of newly arrived tea, prices for previously stored tea have become firm, and ongoing purchases by various firms have resulted in low inventory. An estimated 5,200 boxes of Chun Mei, 1,600 boxes of premium Chun Zhen, and 2,000 boxes of Xiu Mei were sold. Other types such as Gongxi and Xia Mu also performed well. In the past two days, English and European firms have paid close attention to the top-grade Zhuang Shui Dou Chun Mei. Tunxi's famous Chun Mei was offered by Xiehe at 118 yuan, and Zheng Yuan Jia Xin's top-grade Zhuang Chun Mei was offered by European firms at 116 yuan. Zhengxi, known for its excellent craftsmanship, was priced at 90 yuan, and its sub-grade was priced at 70 yuan. The tea market is optimistic about the prospects for Zhuang teas this year. Ping Shui tea and various pearl teas also saw high transaction volumes this week, with Jinlong and Jardine Matheson making substantial purchases totaling 5,000 boxes, and their prices also increased slightly. However, American firms are more critical of the craftsmanship and soup quality of Zhuang teas this year, making it easier to promote high-grade Zhuang teas.

Statistics: June Sesame Export Situation 178

According to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, sesame exports in June totaled 49,970.33 metric tons, an increase of over 7,000 piculs compared to the same month last year. However, the total volume for this year is over 92,000 piculs lower than last year, indicating that sesame exports have not been strong this year. (Unit: metric tons)

Shen Bao Children's Supplement

Plans for Summer Vacation 179

— Xie Yun

Little friends, another year has passed, and it's summer vacation again. You have temporarily left your kind teachers and classmates and returned home. During these long two months, I think you must feel very lonely. Therefore, I am now preparing a summer work plan for you to spend these two months.

The first plan: Publicize the national crisis. The current critical situation of our China has reached a point of extreme urgency. Due to the lack of universal education, the peasants, who account for 50% of the national population, are still unaware of the situation. Little friends, during your summer vacation leisure time, you should organize a small teacher group to publicize the national crisis and methods to save the country to the peasants in the countryside. Your sincere and innocent attitude will surely arouse their enthusiasm for saving the country!

The second plan: Exercise your body. Summer is the time for our outdoor life, and it is also the best opportunity to exercise our body. Cold water baths and ball sports can make our body very healthy. Healthy spirit resides in a healthy body. May little friends not forget this saying!

The third plan: Review old lessons. When summer vacation arrives, your studies have come to an end. When the autumn semester begins, you will step into another new stage. "Reviewing the old can lead to new knowledge." The lessons you have learned in the past are your basic knowledge, and you should review them regularly to become proficient and apply them easily, so you won't feel any difficulty when advancing your studies!

Little friends, please try your best to implement the above three small plans!

The Childhood of Russian Literary Master Gorky 180

— Jun Peng

On the 18th of last month, Russian literary master Gorky passed away in a village near Moscow. Gorky was a Soviet revolutionary literary master and a figure admired by the worldwide cultural community. We were all saddened by his death. Little friends! Brothers and sisters who read the newspaper every day may know that he died of an epidemic, but I will give a brief report on his life during his childhood, and introduce his life story below:

Gorky's father was a carpenter named Maxentius Pescov, and his mother was the daughter of a laundry shop, named Fuffala Gasilin, who lived in Nizhny Novgorod. He was born on March 28, 1868, originally named Alesey Pescov. Later, his family moved to Astrakhan. At the age of five, his father died there, and a younger brother named Wu Hua was born at the same time. Later, his mother remarried. He suffered humiliation at school. When he was ten years old, his mother died. He was then introduced by his grandfather to work as an apprentice in a shoe store. He ran away because he couldn't stand the hardship. He was then recommended by his grandfather to work as a helper in an illustrator's house, and then as an apprentice in a handmade shop. At the age of eleven, he ran away again. At the age of twelve, he wandered to work as a small worker on a Volga River boat, where he met the cook Smolly, who gave him a large number of books to read, and he gained a lot of benefits. Later, he was falsely accused of being a thief by jealous colleagues, and he lost his job again. He returned to the illustrator's house and was beaten. At the age of thirteen, he went to work as an apprentice in an idol shop. At the age of fourteen, he wanted to go to Persia. On the way, he met the former illustrator, who helped him supervise the construction of a house. At the age of fifteen, he went to Kazan, wanting to enter university, but was unsuccessful. He spent a night hungry in a collapsed house in a storm. Later, he worked in a cake shop and attempted suicide with a pistol because of love, injuring his lungs. He recovered after a month. At this time, he realized the truth and went to work as a night watchman at a train station. Later, he worked as a clerk at a lawyer's office. In 1892, at the age of twenty-four, he published his first novel, "MacArthur Chutla," in the local Caucasus Daily, and gradually gained recognition in the literary world under his first single name—Gorky. He served as an editor of tabloids, and his articles gained the sympathy of the general public. During the revolutionary period, he presided over the New Life Daily, and after going through many difficulties, he wrote a total of one hundred and dozens of books, and lived to the age of sixty-eight.

Now he is a member of the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union. Just think about a child from such a poor family who can achieve today's status. Little friends! Gorky is the most outstanding artist; practitioner; enthusiastic revolutionary; and literary master; the most perfect "typical figure" for global people. He is truly a person worthy of admiration and worship!

Monkey 181

— Zhong Mei

Yong'er was "doing nothing but writing large and small characters and flipping through books every day" during the summer vacation. He was very lonely, so he wanted to visit some of his little friends. On this afternoon, the weather was very good. He first went to his friend Min'er's house to play. The two talked and talked very happily. After a while, they walked into Min'er's garden, where chickens, ducks, geese, pigeons, sheep, and cows were raised. In the wooden fence on the left, there were two gray-black monkeys. Yong'er was very happy, so he asked Min'er, "Where did these two monkeys come from? They're so cute!" Min'er replied, "My dad gave them to me. My dad said they are produced in the central part of our country, which is a long way from here."

"Then what do they eat?" "They like to eat fruits and insects and are not carnivores like cats." "What are their teeth like?" "Their teeth are similar to human teeth and can be divided into three types: molars, which have flat and wide tops suitable for grinding food; canines, which have pointed and round shapes suitable for tearing food; and incisors, which have flat shapes suitable for cutting food." "How are they different from humans?" "The differences between them and humans can be summarized as follows: human facial bones are larger than monkey facial bones; human muzzles do not protrude outwards, while monkey muzzles do protrude outwards; humans have no tails, while monkeys have very short tails; and humans do not climb trees, and their buttocks have no calluses or cheek pouches; but monkeys have sharp claws that allow them to climb trees, and their buttocks have calluses and cheek pouches, which are temporary storage places for food." "Then what do they have in common with humans?" "The similarities between them and humans can also be divided into a few points: humans need to be nurtured by the mother's milk, and have four limbs, each with five fingers, with five flat claws, and the forelimbs can grasp objects, and there is a pair of breasts on the chest, and the ear shells are flat, and the brain is very developed. Monkeys also have the same characteristics."

Story Painting 182

— You Jian

——Fun During Summer Vacation

(1) Er'er had nothing to do during the summer vacation, so he wanted to help with the family's production; therefore, he went up the mountain early in the morning to collect firewood. After chopping for a while, he felt tired, so he wanted to take a rest.

(2) Fei'er also wanted to help with the family's production, so he also went to the mountain early in the morning to hunt. He used a rope, so he couldn't catch anything for a long time.

(3) He watched Rong'er sitting and resting in a daze and proudly, and thought to himself: "I'll lasso him!" So he threw the rope over.

(4) Sure enough, Rong'er was lassoed. He tightened the rope and said with a smile, "Caught a person!" He didn't expect that as soon as he finished saying this, he suddenly fell upside down! It turned out that he tightened the rope, and the rope was cut off by the firewood chopping knife!

Happy and Healthy Holiday Life 183

— Sha Ou

Healthy parents can definitely pay attention to cultivating healthy children. Unhealthy parents should pay even more attention to the development of their children's bodies.

In general, parents in middle-class families are busy with their jobs and burdened by family affairs, and they work hard all year round without any holidays. Although schools give long vacations, parents are still unable to spend a leisurely life with their children. How many families can accompany each other to Lushan, Qingdao, Putuo, or Moganshan? Aren't they still confined in that dusty, sultry, and scorching hot cauldron?

Children who are confined to school life all year round should take advantage of their vacations to spend more time outdoors, cultivate a full and healthy spirit, and then continue to work hard on their studies. Parents who work hard all year round should take some time to take their children on a leisurely holiday, restore their tired nerves, rejuvenate their energy for work, and enjoy some family happiness. It is also a way to cultivate a spirit of serving their children and society.

Here are a few healthy rules for holiday life, I hope parents and children themselves pay attention to them!

(1) Do not dress your children up in fancy clothes. Let them wear short shirts and short pants and move, run, and jump freely.

(2) Appropriate camping life is most needed by healthy children. The selection of campsites should pay attention to whether they are suitable for living; whether the location is high and dry; whether the sunlight is sufficient; whether the air is circulated; and whether the supply of drinks and food is convenient.

(3) If you are going to the seaside or lakeside for outdoor life, you should set off early in the morning so that you can enjoy a whole day of rest and recreation.

(4) When resting by the sea, you should not stay too late, and you should not eat too many snacks.

(5) Do not drink well water or spring water casually on the road to prevent unclean sources and cause diarrhea, typhoid fever, and other diseases.

(6) Pay special attention to food. All meats, vegetables, eggs, fruits, milk, etc. must be fresh and clean.

(7) In hot weather, it is not suitable to make excessive hiking trips.

(8) In hot and humid weather, it is not suitable for strenuous exercise.

(9) After settling down, you must plan a regular and varied activity plan.

(10) Driving out is also the most suitable summer life. You can comfortably enjoy the scenery in the wild and breathe fresh air by riding a bicycle or a convertible car.

In this way, we can have a happy, healthy, and meaningful holiday life.

Climbing a Tree to Catch Fish 184

— Dong Xun

Little friends: Doesn't our country have the ancient saying "climbing a tree to catch fish"? However, the facts tell us that there are only birds in the trees, where do the fish come from? So everyone takes this saying as a metaphor!

Unexpectedly, there is such a thing as "climbing a tree to catch fish" in Japan! Beside Daiganji Temple in Soga Town, Chiba Prefecture, there is a very lush forest where there are many black cormorants with long necks and long beaks that build nests in the trees. Cormorants often perch on the branches to rest. Because there are many cormorants in the trees, the ground is covered with cormorant droppings. The children of the nearby residents often go to the forest to collect bird droppings to use as fertilizer for cultivating fields; in addition to picking up bird droppings, they also go there to pick up fish!

I think little friends must be wondering, thinking, how can there be fish in the trees? Isn't this strange? Originally, the forest is close to the sea, and the cormorants in the trees often fly to the sea to catch fish for food; sometimes they stay on the branches, and if they are not careful, the fish will break free from their mouths and fall to the ground, where the children pick them up. Sometimes the children make strange noises or clap their hands to scare them, so that they are frightened and suddenly drop the fish.

Little friends! Don't you think this way of catching fish is very unique and fun?

(Cormorants are a type of waterfowl that is quite skilled at swimming on the water surface to catch fish)

Summer Insect War Exercises 185

— Chen Tiewu

"Cicada?" "Cicada?" The cicada chirps until its lips and tongue are scorched, its propaganda skills are really not small; "Croak! "Croak!" The frog sticks out its white belly, and vigorously beats the war drum; mosquitoes carry barbed knives on their mouths, and flies keep whistling; enemy troops cannot be seen at night, and fireflies light up the electric lights; the dragonfly has a good figure, and performs airplanes to drop bombs; the mantis team dances with large knives; the mole cricket team digs trenches; the ants carry food and grass, working tirelessly all day long; The most gratifying thing is:——the spider's defense is really strict, the electric web is heavily guarded and the enemy cannot escape.

Boy Scout Mailbox

The Brotherhood of Cub Scouts and Wolves——Reply to Zhong Jiabao of Shanghai Guangzhao Girls' School 186

Dear Brother Jiabao:

"Why are Cub Scouts called Wolves?" We believe that many people are as doubtful as you are. It turns out that this novel title was bestowed on us by that old brother Baden-Powell who initiated the Boy Scouts.

In the past, there was a kind of red Indian in America. They had a strange custom: anyone in the tribe who had an independent character, a courageous spirit, a strong physique, and a habit of helping others, the tribe would give him a glorious badge. What is this badge? That's what we didn't expect. This is exactly the "wolf" we are talking about! The black people of Africa also have the same custom. They all like others to call themselves "wolves," and capable children are also called "little wolves." Their "wolves" are just like our Boy Scouts, and are considered to be healthy people. Therefore, our old brother called the Boy Scouts wolves, and the honorable title of "little wolf" was put on the heads of the Cub Scouts.

There is also a very interesting story that describes the story of a missing Indian child living with wild animals in the forest. This child's name is Mao Jili. He was looked after by a mother wolf and lived a wolf's life with the pack. There he learned many forest skills, and a bear and a leopard were his teachers. His life is full of adventures and brave deeds. There is a book that tells this story very interestingly. Our old brother used this book as the basis when he founded the Cub Scouts. Many of the Cub Scouts' activities are similar to the lives of real little wolves, and these little wolf lives are described very interestingly in that book. The book is called The Jungle Book and the author is Kipling.

This is how the Cub Scouts and the Wolves joined hands. In England, you can't find the word "Cub Scout." They are all called little wolves. In China, because there was already the name "Boy Scout," the name "Cub Scout" was followed when "Little Wolf" was held. But even now, the activities of Chinese Cub Scouts are no different from those of foreign little wolves.

Brother Jiabao, what do you think of the name "Little Wolf"? Tell us what you think. Please, I wish you as brave as a wolf!

Sincerely, China Boy Scout Self-Help Society

Children's Creation

I Became a Teacher 187

— Wang Suilan, fifth grader of Dongtai Experimental Elementary School

Time flies so fast. In a blink of an eye, it has been two weeks since the summer vacation started. But after the summer vacation, I became a teacher; it can be said that I have not wasted my precious time.

The sun is setting, and a touch of colorful clouds, like brocade, is swirling in the sky. The evening breeze is blowing gently. At this time, my mother and the aunts from the neighborhood are all gathering in the open space to enjoy the cool air. I took advantage of this time to teach them to recognize common characters. Now they can recognize more than fifty characters.

Little friends all over the country! Let's all get up and make good use of this long summer vacation; and be a teacher like me!

Biography of a Righteous Dog (27) 188

— Xin Qing

A large swath of snow-white light suddenly poured in from the darkness, covering the aisles of the chapel. It turned out that a bright moon had broken through the cloud cover and hung high in the sky. The snow had stopped, and the snow light reflected inside, like the dawn of day. The moonlight shone directly on the two holy images above Little Nello's head, as clear as when he lay down on them during the day.

Little Nello stood up, stretched out his arms towards the two holy images, the happy tear streaks on his pale face shining slightly, he shouted loudly: "I finally see them! Ah! God! I am completely satisfied."

His two legs finally couldn't support him. He knelt on the ground, his eyes still looking up at the two holy images he loved. The moonlight lingered on the holy images for a moment, particularly bright, particularly clear, particularly sweet and intense, as if shot down from heaven to make it convenient for Little Nello. Suddenly, the bright light disappeared again, and darkness covered the face of Jesus Christ.

Little Nello's arms tightened around Patrasche's body, and he murmured: "Let's go up and see his face again. I don't think he will separate us again, he is the most merciful."

The next day, the citizens of Antwerp found Little Nello and Patrasche next to the altar of the Great Church. They were both dead. The cold night air had frozen them both stiff, like stones. On this Christmas morning, when the priests came to the temple, they saw them lying on the stone steps of the altar. Above them, the curtain on the holy image of Ruben had been unveiled, and beams of sunlight were shining directly on the head of God.

Later, a stern-faced old man arrived, and seeing many women crying, he also sobbed and cried, murmuring, "I really mistreated this child. I must try my best to make up for it and repent of my sins in the future. Even though he is dead, I must still treat him as my own son."

Later, a world-famous old painter arrived and said to the crowd, "I am looking for a very talented child. The prize money from yesterday should be awarded to him. He painted an old woodcutter sitting on a fallen tree when the sunset was beautiful. Although this is a very simple painting, it can be seen that he has a great future. I wholeheartedly want to find him and teach him art wholeheartedly, and I will get the greatest harvest."

There was also a blonde girl, holding her father's arm, crying very sadly, shouting, "Ah! Nello! Come on! We have everything prepared for you. We have a lot of Christmas gifts. That old musician will also play the flute for us to add to the fun; mother also said she would let you stay and go back after the festival, then Patrasche will be so happy! Ah! Nello! Wake up quickly! Come with us"!

But Little Nello's pale face, looking up at the bright light on the holy image of Ruben, had a hint of a smile on his mouth, as if answering their words: "It's too late"!

Sweet bells were ringing on a cold day, the sunlight was shining on the snowy plains. The citizens were walking in the streets in teams happily, but Little Nello and Patrasche would no longer come to beg from them.

They were always together in life, and they would not be separated after death. Because people saw that the child's arms were tightly holding the dog's body, no one could separate them. The people in this small village were very ashamed and regretful, and they specially held a prayer service for them, and built a grave to lay them together—to sleep forever. (The End)

Supplement to Shen Bao This City - Amateur Weekly

Amateur Study

How to Study Mathematics? 189

— De Zhao

Our world is a world of matter; matter is composed of quantities, and therefore it can also be said that this world is a world of numbers. We see that the mountains and rivers of the natural world each have their own size, height, or length, all containing many substances and many quantities of substances. Looking at human society, the composition of countries and groups inevitably involves many members, and all production and consumption of people inevitably have certain quantities. At some point, we can say that all phenomena can be explained by numbers. As for our lives, they can be even more calculated with numbers, such as how much we earn and spend each month, how many hours we work and read each day, and how much time we rest. It can be said that everything can be calculated with numbers. The general terms arithmetic and mathematics are used to calculate phenomena related to the natural world, human society, and individual lives. They have real content and a material basis. Each number or digit can represent the quantity of something. For example, two plus three equals five, which is the representation of five people, five hours, five dollars, or five somethings. We can say that all numbers have real content; otherwise, they would not have any meaning.

Because quantity is contained within things themselves, and the foundation of mathematics is objective reality, and humans cannot live without objective reality, the learning of mathematics is definitely not for simple exams but is of great benefit to our real lives. Studying mathematics is for the sake of gaining more mathematical knowledge to help us live. On a small scale, such as our daily lives, if we can use mathematical knowledge to plan production and consumption, it will be much better than living a muddled, anarchic life. As the saying goes, "You won't get poor from wearing or eating, but you'll deserve to be poor if you don't know how to calculate!" This is a satire on those who cannot use arithmetic knowledge to live. On a large scale, no matter what subject you study or what matter you handle, if you have rich arithmetic knowledge, it can not only make your mind clear and organized but also have many practical benefits in your research or handling of affairs.

So, how to study mathematics? Here, we can briefly list a few points:

First, to study mathematics, it is necessary to study new social sciences and philosophy because mathematical knowledge can only be used flexibly and can only progress if you have new ideas. We often see many mathematicians who have a very rich mathematical knowledge but whose minds are mechanically dead and unable to do anything. You know, in history, no, even now, aren't there many mathematicians and natural scientists who are superstitious about God? This is clearly a contradictory expression of their scientific and mathematical knowledge. But the root of this contradiction lies in the fact that they only know how to draw X×Y or 1/3 or 2+3 and other mathematical formulas every day and don't care about anything else. As a result, they don't know anything else either, developing a rigid brain. For such mathematicians, new knowledge is certainly not easily accepted. For example, the theory of relativity is considered absurd by most mathematicians, but in fact, this theory is the most progressive. In the eyes of mathematicians with rigid brains who have no new ideas, four of course is only equal to four and nothing else, but in reality, the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan was completed in four years. The content of this four is five. But isn't this an incomprehensible statement to mechanical mathematicians?

Second, since mathematics is of great use to our real lives, we should pay special attention to its practicality when studying it and not study mathematics for the sake of mathematics. It is said that in 212 BC, when Roman soldiers broke through the city of Syracuse, the scientist Archimedes was still drawing and studying on the sand in a small house. When soldiers entered his house, he was still saying, "Do not destroy my circle!" This is a common example used by our quietists when "admonishing" general young students. In my opinion, the scientist's spirit of research is certainly very good, but we dare not agree with such a tendency. Because the enemy soldiers have already entered the city, the country is destroyed, and the family is ruined. Even one's own life cannot be protected. Even if his circle is successfully drawn and his research has great achievements, what use is it? Because of this, we advise friends who are learning mathematics not to just bury themselves in XY or one, two, three, four, etc. You must pay attention to national and social issues at all times, and you must always think about the practical use of your knowledge. Think about it, in the current situation in China, even if you learn mathematics well, can you use it to develop industry in China? Can you use it to save the country? I'm afraid at most you'll just end up being a comprador eating foreign food.

Third, to study mathematics, it is necessary to pay attention to your daily life at all times, and it is even more necessary to think deeply. When a math problem is placed before your eyes, you should spend more time thinking about it. Do not mechanically use mathematical formulas, immediately pick up a pen and start calculating, nor should you give up completely because you cannot do it for a while. I once saw a student learning mathematics encounter the following problem: A gentleman hired a nanny, stating that the monthly salary was eight yuan. Now the nanny only worked for eighteen days. How much should the salary be? For this question, he used the usual arithmetic rules, first dividing eight yuan by thirty days, trying to find the nanny's daily salary, and then multiplying the quotient by eighteen. Wouldn't the result be the nanny's salary for eighteen days? Little did he know that dividing eight by thirty can never be divided completely, which made it impossible to solve. But if you could think about it carefully, this question is very easy to answer. First, you should think that thirty days is eight yuan, then three days should be eight jiao. Then think that eighteen days is six three-day periods. So, eight multiplied by six equals forty-eight. This is the nanny's salary for eighteen days, which is forty-eight jiao, or four yuan and eight jiao. Another example is that there are six sparrows on a tree. You shoot at them, and one sparrow is hit and falls to the ground. How many sparrows are left on the tree? If you answer without thinking that there are five sparrows left on the tree, you are wrong because the five sparrows that were not hit have already flown away at the sound of the gunshot. In fact, there are no sparrows left on the tree. There are many mathematical problems like this that require careful thought, and I hope researchers will pay attention at all times.

Fourth, for abstract mathematical formulas, it is necessary to assume their concrete content to think about them, which makes them easier to understand.

Finally, of course, you have to spend more time learning. In particular, you should not be afraid of difficulties and do more exercises because this can enrich your knowledge and make your calculations proficient.

The Scenery of Shanghai

Summer at the Takahashi Seaside Bathing Beach 190

— De Zhao

Since China produced the mermaid, the summer entertainment and sports trend has shifted to swimming

Page 22

, and besides, there are many people who want to eat ice cream with their eyes! Therefore, every summer, the swimming pools in Shanghai are overcrowded. Not only are those who can swim shoulder to shoulder in the water, but there are also many who sit and watch from the sidelines without getting into the water. However, the capacity of small swimming pools is limited, and people get tired of seeing them after a long time. Therefore, the Takahashi Seaside Bathing Beach has become a reality in the imaginations of many people.

I remember before the Takahashi Seaside Bathing Beach appeared, I was attracted by an advertisement to a so-called "Ming Garden" Seaside Bathing Beach. It was an entertainment venue surrounded by factory areas near Yangshupu. The so-called seaside was just a pile of sand next to an ordinary swimming pool, with a few large umbrellas propped up, and a large-scale seascape painted on the wall of the house across the street. This kind of advertising seaside makes people laugh or cry after you get there.

After all, Shanghai is a place where culture and talents gather, so it is finally possible to enjoy a real seawater bath, and the name Takahashi becomes active in the eyes of a group of people who love swimming and sightseeing every summer. Speaking of Takahashi, the road is not too far; it is on the opposite bank of Wusong. But the transportation is still convenient, with special city ferry boats and public buses specially prepared for tourists. There are also artificially improved beaches and gardens, ponds, embankments, pavilions, and other arrangements, allowing tourists to rest.

Although the shocking waves of the sea can give people a terrifying imagination, the vastness and clarity of the sea, the endlessness, the misty water and sky, and the clear and refreshing breeze often give people a beautiful and warm feeling, making you linger and reluctant to leave. And the Takahashi Seaside is like this. There is an endless beach with miles of flat sand. Under the blue sky, white waves, and strong sunlight, there are scattered tents like Mongolian yurts. You can bring friends and sit on the sand in the tent with cool mats, looking into the distance. It is simply impossible to distinguish the continent from the sky, only vaguely seeing the sails in the distance and sparse islands. Breathing in the air is like drinking nectar. In the early morning and near dusk, when the scorching sun has no energy, you feel the cool breeze and the water is calm. At that time, you can take off your clothes and shoes and swim or walk, which will make you forget the heat and stuffiness and make you feel that there is no summer this year. At the same time, there is also a benefit on the beach, that is, the water there is active. Although you sit not far from the water, the water, activated by the tide, will be sent to your sides in bursts. Sometimes there are one or two small waves, like fountains spraying to your head, face, and body, scattering like pearls, with a posture that is both beautiful and charmingly gentle. Moreover, this method of waiting for the water is extremely suitable for people who are not good at swimming! Everyone should also pay attention: If you lack strength, it is best not to slide into the sea. Because the running water is merciless. The powerful waves and the soft sand often trap you without you realizing it!

The route to get there is to first go to the City Ferry Terminal on the Bund of Beijing Road (next to the famous "Floating Hotel"), where a ferry departs every hour. The round-trip ferry fee, if you take second-class seats, is six jiao and eight fen, and you can buy　　　. The ferry departs from Shanghai and breaks through the waves straight ahead in the Huangpu River. The river wind constantly blows against your clothes, making you forget the heat. If you take first-class seats, it is even more "xieyi." There are canvas chairs on the deck, and you can sit comfortably and lean back. After the blurred buildings on both sides and the clear foreign warships and merchant ships in the river gradually drift westward, you can see the green embankments of Jun Gong Road and the fields of Pudong. After passing Xidu, Donggou, Qingningsi and other places, the ferry docks at the Takahashi Ferry Terminal. There, public buses have been waiting. You can take the bus with your ticket, pass through Takahashi Town and the green fields on both sides, and arrive at the Takahashi Seaside in less than half an hour. Although the road is narrow, it is not flat, and it is winding and full of fun. After getting off the bus, you will see the gate of the Seaside Bathing Beach. After entering the gate, stepping on the stone steps, and passing the ticket office, you can see the artificially arranged garden: it is like a "吕" character shape, a large pond, with an embankment in the middle dividing it into two, and a pavilion on top. On the surrounding embankments, green trees are lush, with lush branches and leaves, thriving. It is said that the water in this pond is fresh water, and tourists can wash again with fresh water in the pond after taking a seawater bath to remove the salt. A row of elegant thatched houses, similar to old-style hall buildings, are called Thatched Halls. There is also a large dining hall, called the Seaside Dining Hall, which offers noodles, wine, and dishes. The Thatched Halls offer various cold drinks. From here to the east is the beach. To the north, countless tents are propped up, gathering hundreds of male and female tourists. On the higher ground is the building of the so-called "Seaside Hotel," where you can stay for the summer. A touch of green gauze on the doors and windows makes the tourists inside look like they are living in the clouds.

Places to rent swimsuits, tents, and rubber floats are available, and the cost is not very high. Healthy and beautiful people are wriggling on the beach, and the number of women is no less than that of men. A gust of sea breeze blows from the ground, and we can hear the laughter and the sound of the tide echoing in our ears.

There, it is indeed a moving summer picture. Scenery, people, and nature are all available!

Literary Works

Diary from the Back Building (Continued and Finished) 191

— Shu Yu

September 25th

This morning, the landlady asked about the situation of Company A in her conversation. I had to fabricate some things casually and managed to muddle through.

Thank goodness! Mr. Ji gave me good news. The letter only contained three or two simple sentences, saying, "Please come to work at the company on the 26th." I couldn't help but cry! I don't know if these are tears of gratitude or tears of sadness?

From tomorrow on, I really have to go to Company A to handle affairs, but I will be too busy to keep this diary. Let's wait until the next time I'm unemployed—I believe such a time will come again—to continue writing.

Don't forget! Tomorrow is September 26th. (The End)

Starting yesterday (Saturday), "Uncle Yu Lai," a new-style dance partner, will continue to perform new dance skills in the revolving hall of the International Hotel in this city.

Humorous Sketch

The Officials on the Deserted Island 192

— Translated by Zhen Jie

Once upon a time, in the old Russian era, there were two officials, both of whom were brainless. One day, they suddenly felt that they had been sent to a deserted island without human habitation, as if they were sitting on the magic carpet in "The Arabian Nights."

They had spent their entire lives in the Records Department of the Ministry of Government Affairs, where they were born, raised, and grew up. Therefore, they knew nothing about anything outside the "Ministry." All they knew was only one sentence, which was: "Respectfully presented to His Excellency So-and-So, Your Excellency, Your Servant So-and-So respectfully presents."

But this Ministry of Government Affairs was later abolished, and the positions of the two officials were no longer needed. They were dismissed and were idle.

Page 23

Therefore, these two retired officials moved to Cheskaya Street in St. Petersburg. They each had their own families, their own cooks, and their own retirement pensions.

When they suddenly woke up on a deserted island without human habitation, they found themselves lying under the sky. At first, of course, they didn't understand what had happened to them. They were both surprised and asked, "Good heavens! What does this mean? Where are we?"

They touched and pinched each other to confirm that it was not a dream. Finally, they admitted this sad reality. They felt that in front of them was a vast ocean, behind them was only a little bit of land, and after that little bit of land was another ocean. They started crying—this cry can be said to be the first cry since their "Ministry" closed its doors. At the same time, they looked at each other and saw that neither of them was wearing much except pajamas and a medal hanging on their heads.

"Is it time for coffee now?" one of the officials said. He thought and cried: "What should we do now? Even if we draft a submission, what's the use!"

"You know, Your Excellency!" another official cheered up and said: "You go to the east, and I'll go to the west. When we all return to the original place, maybe we will find something."

They then set about distinguishing which direction was east and which direction was west. They remembered that once the minister had said to them: "If you want to know where the east is, then turn your face to the north, and the east will be on your right hand." But when they wanted to find out which side was north, they could only turn right, turn left, and look around in all directions. Because they had spent their entire lives in the Document Section, their efforts were all in vain.

"I think, Your Excellency! The best way is for you to go to the right and I'll go to the left!" one of the officials said. He had not only worked in the Document Section but also taught calligraphy at the preparatory military school, so he was a little smarter.

As they said, so they did. One of the officials walked to the right. He came across many trees full of various fruits. He really wanted to pick an apple, but they were all hanging high on the branches, forcing him to climb up. He climbed around and failed. All he could do was tear his pajamas. Walking to a stream, he saw countless fish swimming in the deep water. Entering the forest, he saw many crows and wild rabbits, etc. He drooled. "Good heavens, there are so many things to eat!" he shouted, and the fire of hunger burned even more. But he finally returned to the agreed place empty-handed.

"How is it, Your Excellency? Did you find anything?"

"No, just an old Moscow newspaper!"

The two officials lay down again, but their empty stomachs did not allow them to rest. Half of their sleepy eyes were seeing those people who were enjoying a happy life on their pensions; the other half were disturbed by the fresh fruits, fish, birds, and wild rabbits they had seen during the day, making them unable to settle down.

"The things that humans eat, their original forms are flying in the sky, swimming in the water, and growing on trees. Who would have thought of that? Your Excellency!"

"That's right!" another official continued: "I must also admit; I always thought that the bread and butter we eat for breakfast were born into the world just like they are on the plates on the table."

"According to this reasoning, then, if we want to eat a pheasant, we must catch it, kill it, pluck its feathers, and roast it, but how do we start? The two said in unison.

They fell silent and tried to fall asleep again, but hunger always drove sleep away.

"I believe I can eat my own boots right now!" one of the officials said again, cheering up.

"Leather gloves aren't bad either, especially if they've been softened!" another official said.

The two officials glared at each other intently. Their eyes radiated like flames; their teeth were chattering. A turbid moan came from their chests. They slowly approached, suddenly becoming like terrible madmen. They shouted, roared, and burned with anger. The official who had been a calligraphy teacher pounced on him and bit off his colleague's badge, swallowing it into his stomach. It was not until his teeth saw blood that their consciousness returned.

"God save us!" they shouted at the same time: "We must not eat each other!"

They were silent again for a while.

"In any case, we must say something to pass the time. Otherwise, murder and death will happen!" one of the officials said.

"Can you explain why the sun rises first and then sets? Why not reverse it?"

"Aren't you a funny person? You get up first! Your Excellency! Then you go to the department to work, um um... then you have to eat dinner!" He stared and dared not go on.

"But why doesn't man reverse it? You can sleep first, see the things in your dreams, and then get up!"

"Ah, that's right. But when I was an official, I always thought: now it's dawn, then it will soon be day, um um... then it will be dinner!" He blurted it out again. But saying the word "dinner" reminded them of their experiences during the day, and the two officials became sad. They were silent for a while again.

"A doctor told me that a person can support himself with his own spirit for a long time," one of the officials began again.

"What does that mean?"

"It's very simple. You know, a person's own essence and blood produce other essence and blood, and the other circulates and produces another kind of essence and blood. This goes on until all the essence and blood are gone."

"What happens after that?"

"After that, you have to put something to eat in your stomach!"

"This devil!" the other official cried.

No matter what issue they talked about, the result invariably turned to "eating." This only made their appetite even stronger. Therefore, they decided not to talk about anything. They thought of the old Moscow newspaper that they had picked up, and the other official began to read:

"A Record of the Grand Feast of the Governor! Delicious delicacies from land and sea!"

"Devil! Please don't read any more!" the other official cried out with a desperate expression. He snatched the newspaper from his colleague and began to find something else to read:

"Our correspondent from Tula writes that yesterday, a sturgeon was obtained near the Upa River, which is rare in the local area, so a banquet was held to celebrate it. The main course was placed in a large wooden basin, decorated with pickled melons and fruits, and a sprig of parsley was inserted into the fish's mouth. Each guest received a piece. The cooking was exceptionally exquisite!..."

"I'm sorry, Your Excellency! I don't think you are good at choosing reading material either?" So the official who interrupted the conversation snatched the newspaper again and read:

"A certain old resident of Vitek has recently invented a novel recipe for making fish soup..."

The heads of the two officials drooped. No matter where their eyes looked, it was something related to eating. Their thoughts were also destined to think about eating. No matter how hard they tried not to think about steaks or the like, everything was in vain. Their fantasies were invariably without room for resistance and would return to the things they painfully wailed about. Finally, one of the officials had an inspiration:

"I've thought of a way!" he cried happily. "Your Excellency! What do you think? We can go find a farmer!"

"Ah, a farmer, but how can we catch one?"

"There must be one here, because this thing is everywhere."

So they walked around on the deserted island for a long time, and finally they found a farmer sleeping under a tree.

"What? Sleeping here? You lazybones!" they scolded the farmer angrily: "Two officials are about to starve to death, and you don't care? Get up! Go! Go to work!"

The farmer got up and saw these two angry gentlemen standing in front of him. At first, he wanted to escape. But the two officials suddenly caught him, and he had to submit to his fate. He had to obey the two officials and go to work for them.

He first climbed up the tree and picked dozens of good apples for the two officials, leaving a bad one for himself. Later, he used a wooden drill to make fire, and he plucked his own hair to make a net to catch some crows and rabbits. He used his fire to roast these delicious wild game, allowing the two officials to eat comfortably and relieve their hunger.

The two officials were very happy to see that the farmer was able to work hard. They had already forgotten how close they were to starving to death yesterday! They were only thinking about how to be an official who could rule and drive this farmer.

World News

Fish Eyes Mixed with Pearls 193

— Dongyuan

There was a French actress named Madame Solaire. In 1933, she was already seventy years old, but thanks to the art of makeup, when she appeared on stage, she still looked beautiful and was admired by all.

Unfortunately, however, the wrinkles on this beautiful actress's face had recently become too obvious, and even the most skillful makeup could not hide them. Therefore, she was filled with sorrow, feeling that her youth had passed! But she was not discouraged and still wanted to use the power of science to restore her youth. She found a famous doctor, Dr. Asterley, and paid him 10,000 gold francs to remove her wrinkles. As a result, thanks to the doctor's excellent surgery, the wrinkles on the old actress's face were indeed removed, but she did not fulfill the contract and refused to pay the doctor the 10,000 gold francs for the surgery. The doctor was not satisfied and eventually filed a lawsuit in court.

When this news spread, the general Parisian public was very surprised. When the trial began, many people went to listen in. The defendant, Madame Solaire, also appeared in court in person. When the judge asked her why she had violated the contract, she immediately argued: "Although the wrinkles around my eyes disappeared as a result of the doctor's surgery, my eyes have become like fish eyes. Not only can I not look around freely, but I cannot even close them. Should I still pay the surgery fee?" But the doctor said: "The contract was for me to remove your wrinkles. Now that the wrinkles have been removed, no matter what, the contract should be fulfilled." What was the result? The doctor's lawsuit was ultimately dismissed.

Current Affairs Research

Unstable British Diplomacy 194

— Diqiu

In the recent Montreux Conference, Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu bluntly accused the British delegation: "You advocate one policy in Geneva and another here. You are trying your best to undermine mutual assistance and regional agreements!" This is a ruthless yet appropriate criticism of Britain's recent diplomatic attitude. In fact, because the British Empire has the most territories and the largest sphere of influence, it has conflicts with all countries in the world, large or small. And because the British Empire is in decline and everything tends to be conservative, it has failed to adopt a resolute foreign policy towards other countries. As a result, London's diplomatic activities have become unstable.

Not to mention distant events, let's just look at recent facts. For example, when London suddenly felt that Hitler's actions posed a danger to it, British imperialism immediately united with France and Italy to form the Stresa Front against Germany. But just as this front was forming, it felt that it should not help France to contain Germany, so it turned around and negotiated with Berlin, concluding the Anglo-German Naval Agreement. Regarding Italy, in the past, Britain wanted to maintain friendly relations with it, but unfortunately, Mussolini wanted to monopolize Abyssinia, threatening British rights in Africa and the Mediterranean, making it unable to adopt a positive attitude towards Italy for a time. As a result, London's diplomats became busy, constantly shuttling between Paris, Geneva, and London, resolutely advocating sanctions against Italy. At the same time, the Far East fleet was also transferred to the Mediterranean, and it even threatened to close the Suez Canal. For a time, commentators said that Britain had adopted a positive attitude. However, after the Italian army achieved a temporary victory in its invasion of Abyssinia, the old British imperialism, seeing that the source of the Nile River was not being affected, and also feeling that Mussolini was arrogant and invincible, had no choice but to disregard its reputation and voluntarily proposed the lifting of sanctions against Italy in Geneva and began to transfer the Mediterranean fleet back to its original defenses in order to appease Mussolini. At the Montreux Conference, when the Soviet Union requested that the Black Sea Fleet be allowed to freely enter the Mediterranean and advocated the wartime blockade of the Black Sea, it was generally believed that this was to prevent the development of German and Italian aggression, and Britain would likely agree. However, London's diplomats felt that this would threaten British power in the Mediterranean, so they desperately opposed the Soviet Union's proposal, leading to the Romanian Foreign Minister's rebuke. These facts have all occurred recently, and therefore they can all prove that even now British diplomacy is still continuing to waver.

Such British diplomacy is of course very welcome in Italy and Germany. Hitler, under London's hesitant attitude and secret encouragement, rearmed, tearing up the Versailles and Locarno Treaties. Italy's invasion of Abyssinia was opposed by Britain, but it was also British imperialism that first recognized the results of this invasion. Now, Italy and Germany have formed a common front, which is the establishment of the German-Austrian rapprochement agreement.

According to the Berlin and Vienna communiqués, the terms of the German-Austrian agreement are:

(1) Germany recognizes Austria's full sovereignty;

(2) Each country agrees not to directly or indirectly interfere in the other's internal political development, including the issue of Austrian National Socialism;

(3) Austria intends to maintain a special policy towards Germany in accordance with the basic principles of Austria's recognition of itself as a German state, so as not to disturb the Roman Protocol of 1934 and the Additional Articles of 1936, and the status of Italy, Austria, and Hungary as parties to this document.

At the same time, the Austrian cabinet has been reorganized, with the famous pro-German element, Hossbach, appointed as a Minister without Portfolio, and Schmidt as Foreign Minister. In this way, the long-standing dispute that had not been improved between Germany and Austria has now become friendly. This friendship has further promoted the combination of Germany and Italy, forming a Central European bloc centered on Germany and Italy and including Poland and Austria-Hungary. Because Poland has always followed Berlin, and Austria-Hungary has long been under Rome's control, and Germany's main conflict in the past was the Austrian issue, now that German-Austrian relations have improved, Germany and Italy can of course immediately combine, and thus Poland and Austria-Hungary will inevitably become more subordinate to these two major aggressor countries, forming a Central European aggression bloc. When the German-Austrian rapprochement agreement was announced, from Rome to Warsaw, they were all expressing rejoicing. Regarding the meeting of the signatories of the Locarno Treaty and the East African issue, Hitler and Mussolini both expressed the same attitude in unison. All of this can be said to be the spiritual manifestation of the formation of the Central European bloc.

Naturally, we cannot say that this Central European aggression bloc was entirely promoted by unstable British diplomacy, but in recent years, the reckless actions of Germany and Italy, regardless of everything, are also closely related to the wavering London diplomacy. We can say that if Britain could resolutely fulfill its obligations under international treaties, world peace would at least not be threatened as much as it is now, and the reckless actions of Germany and Italy would at least have some reservations.

Now that Europe's two major dangerous countries have combined, and Poland and Austria-Hungary are even more attached to them, their adventurous behavior will of course be even more severe in the future, and the guarantee of peace in Europe and even the world will of course be more problematic. In this situation, the first to be threatened are France, the Soviet Union, and the Little Entente, which of course have no direct relationship with the British Empire and do not require it to worry. Moreover, to be honest, London's diplomats are actually very happy to see the emergence of the German-Italian bloc to stand against the French-Soviet bloc, because once this situation is created, Britain can sit in the middle and benefit from the struggle. Therefore, British public opinion expressed "relief" after the German-Austrian agreement was announced. However, if Germany, following the resolution of the Austrian issue, suddenly very practically raises the issue of recovering pre-war colonies, then the German colonies formerly administered by Britain in Africa, Australia, and other places would be in immediate danger of being taken back. At that time, Britain would probably have to adopt a positive attitude to maintain the status quo. And if Italy, with the help of Germany, continues to expand its power in Africa and the Mediterranean, then London would probably have to raise the slogan of sanctions again. But when the unfortunate events for Britain really come again, the so-called temporary positive attitude will really not be of much use. When the Italian-Abyssinian War had already broken out and the situation in the Far East was even more serious, what effect did the temporary positive attitude adopted by Britain have? If Britain wants to truly obtain temporary security, it should prepare to cooperate with France and the Soviet Union to use the power of the group to stop all aggressive and adventurous actions. According to reports, Soviet figures recently criticized Britain, saying, "Those who advocate maintaining the European status quo must unite with each other at this moment to resist Germany's policy of external development. And for the sake of British interests, it is also advisable to join this group, otherwise the matter of surrender will be staged again and again, and Hitler, the leader of Germany, will advance even more recklessly and unscrupulously! Moreover, the agreement between Germany and Austria is actually the natural result of Germany's unilateral abolition of the Locarno Treaty and the restoration of armed forces in the Rhineland region. According to this, the country has the possibility of invading Central Europe in order to form a strong group to isolate Eastern Europe from Western Europe." We believe that such remarks are worthy of consideration by London's diplomats.

However, judging from the current situation, Britain under the Conservative Party cabinet will probably not adopt a positive attitude to maintain the status quo. It will continue its wavering diplomatic policy: today it will use France to contain Germany and Italy, and tomorrow it will support Germany and Italy to resist the French-Soviet bloc, on the one hand making friends with all countries, and on the other hand contradicting all countries. In this way, aggressors are allowed to advance boldly under Britain's moderation and cover, so as to disrupt peace, and at the same time, it will turn around and endanger Britain.

Today's Europe, Britain is in a pivotal position between two major hostile blocs, namely the French-Soviet bloc and the German-Italian bloc. If it can combine with France and the Soviet Union, then Germany and Italy's outward development will naturally be strongly hindered. Conversely, if it participates in or even leads the German-Italian bloc to confront France and the Soviet Union, then European peace will immediately become a problem. But Britain does not adopt a resolute attitude. It hopes that others will engage in war, especially that this war will move to Eastern Europe and erupt in Ukraine, so that it can benefit from it without any loss. However, the development of events is not necessarily in line with London's thinking. Not to mention other things, if the conflict between the French-Soviet and German-Italian blocs develops to the point of armed conflict, or if German-Italian forces have a direct conflict with Britain in the Balkans, in the Mediterranean, or in Africa, then its intermediate position in the European situation and its unstable diplomatic policy will necessarily be automatically canceled.

Fragments

Random Mix from the Dunmeng Stone Room 195

— Mengfei

The "Historical Records: Wu Family" records: "When Zixu was about to die, he said: 'Gouge out my eyes and place them on the east gate of Wu, to watch the Yue destroy Wu.'" His gnashing of teeth and festering heart were like this. I cannot help but feel sad for today's quasi-slaves of a ruined nation.

Wang Ruoxu said: "There are three mistakes in interpreting the Analects: being too profound, being too lofty, and being too generous. The words of the sages are also human emotions." For those who blindly believe in the classics, this is a wake-up call!

"If one has not been heard of at forty or fifty, then one is not to be feared." "If one is hated at forty, then one's end is near." People do have those who change their principles late in life, but generally speaking, one can also see that their ends are different.

"Learning then not firm." "Firm" should be interpreted as "obscured." If interpreted as "strong," then there is a difference as vast as between a hair and a thousand miles.

The relationship between father and son is different now and in the past. In the past, Confucius said: "Not changing the way of one's father for three years, one can be said to be filial!" In fact, what can be changed need not wait three years, and what cannot be changed cannot be changed even for a lifetime.

Lu Yushu's poem says: "Learning is like Yuan Kai, becoming an addiction, writing is like Xiangru, resembling a wanderer, standing alone at Confucius's door, nothing to do, losing to Yanzi, his mind is dedicated." This praises Yanzi's joy in his humble alley.

Fan Chunfu said: "The gentleman studies his inner self, the petty man pursues his outer self. What the gentleman governs is the root, what the petty man governs is the branches." This is the watershed between gentlemen and petty men.

Emperor Xizong of Tang blamed the concubines of Huang Chao for following the rebels. One replied: "The state, with a million troops, lost its ancestral temples and fled to Bazhong. Now you blame a woman for not being able to resist the rebels. Where do you place the dukes, ministers, generals, and commanders?" Reading these words, thinking of the treason of Yin Rugeng and others, I cannot help but feel sad for a long time.
